\- Version 6.03 doesn't contain any important new features.  
   
**New functions and fixes in Total Commander 6.02:**  
   
\- Version 6.02 doesn't contain any important new features.  
   
**New functions and fixes in Total Commander 6.01:**  
   
\- Version 6.01 doesn't contain any new features.  
   
**New functions and fixes in Total Commander 6.0:**  
   
\- Supports Unicode file names when Copying/Moving/Renaming files  
\- Comparison of Unicode-Text files in "Compare by Content"  
\- Folder Tabs for quickly switching between folders  
\- Ctrl+T now used for the new Tabs, Ctrl+M for the Multi-Rename Tool  
\- Regular Expressions for Searching, Multi-Rename Tool, Copying etc.  
\- Separate buttons for Directory Hotlist and History  
\- Speed display when copying  
\- Copy function configurable via Settings dialog.  
\- F2 in the copy dialog adds the files to the background transfer manager  
\- Options button in the copy dialog allows to rename copied or target files automatically on identical name  
\- Speed limit in the background transfer manager now also works when copying  
\- Synchronize dirs now tries to set the date/time of FTP files via MDTM command (not working with all servers)  
\- Synchronize dirs: Now also with archives other than ZIP  
\- Support for accents in domains for FTP and HTTP  
\- Multiple new internal commands, like cm\_copySamepanel, cm\_copyOtherpanel, cm\_createShortcuts, cm\_SaveSelection, cm\_ShowHint  
\- Show sequence number in the program title if multiple Total Commander open  
\- Drive button icons can be replaced via external DLL  
\- Configuration dialog uses a list instead of tab headers  
\- FTP: Resume all  
\- Wait in the background for external packers  
\- Double click on \[..\] in the root leads to "My Computer" (configurable)  
\- Environment variable COMMANDER\_PATH now points to the Total Commander directory  
   
**New functions and fixes in Total Commander 5.51:**  
   
\- A click on the currently active path allows to edit or copy/paste it  
\- Include/exclude certain directories in [search function](#bookmark=id.yr4hyk5v9h95)  
\- Search and synchronize dirs now also work with file system plugins  
\- Support for [Lister plugins](#bookmark=id.5ezopyc2176e)  
\- Support for custom icons in file system plugins  
\- Deleting of non-empty directories on SAMBA drives sometimes failed  
\- Moved OLE comment retrieval to a separate thread (background), because it can be slow for some file types  
\- Couldn't view RTF file currently open in Word (sharing problem)  
\- Support for internal commands in Ctrl+D menu ([directory hotlist](#bookmark=id.56m1msgg5onh)), e.g. cm\_OpenDesktop  
\- Limited Unicode support in file names: Delete, Rename, View, Edit and Show properties  
   
**New functions in Total Commander 5.50:**  
   
\- Name changed to "Total Commander" \- see our homepage for the reasons  
\- Change size display of total/marked files in footer below file lists (bytes, k or dynamic)  
\- Copy additional NTFS streams when copying files.  
\- Copy file comments with the files with F5 (optional, needs to be enabled first)  
\- Create CRC checksums: Function can now also create and check MD5 checksums  
\- Drag a link from Internet Explorer to Total Commander (holding down Shift) to open the URL dialog to download the linked file  
\- File system plugin interface to access external devices or other partitions  
\- In Copy dialog, "Options" button which allows to set "Overwrite all", "Skip all" etc. before copying  
\- Lister: In 'Fit to window' mode, resize the video window to the lister window  
\- Lister: RTF-Viewer (can be disabled)  
\- Multi-rename tool: Load/Save settings, for often used changes  
\- Multi-rename tool, search+replace: Support for wildcards \* and ?  
\- Open partially downloaded ZIP files, even during the download  
\- Option: Always open new FTP connections in the left or right file panel instead of the active file panel  
\- Show file comments in file lists and as tooltips  
\- Show name of logged-on user in the title bar if the program was started with RunAs  
\- Synchronize dirs, asymmetric mode: Option to delete all empty dirs in right window (not available in zip or ftp)  
\- The HTML viewer in Lister supports some more tags  
   
**New functions in Commander 5.10:**  
   
\- Unpack RAR 3 archives  
\- Support for OTP-MD4 \-MD5 and \-SHA1-authentication for FTP  
\- Decoder for Yenc-encoded files (Files \- decode files)  
   
**New functions in Commander 5.01:**  
   
**\-** Unpack RAR 3 archives  
\- Support for OTP-MD4 and \-MD5-authentication for FTP  
   
**New functions in Commander 5.00:**  
   
**\-** Support for Windows XP themes on XP  
**\-** "Commands" menu split into "Commands" and "Net"  
**\-** FTP: support for more than 2 definition strings when [defining a new server type](#bookmark=id.r5cp5ajvcrzy)  
\- [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7)\+HTTP: Auto-Resume download if download-connection lost  
\- FTP: SOCKS4+SOCKS5 [Proxy](#bookmark=id.3qo1eirdd3lq) support (active+passive mode\!), SOCKS5 without encryption  
\- [Multi-Rename-Tool](#bookmark=id.rx16tlz9efm5): Placeholder \[P\] puts name of parent dir into file name  
\- Internal command cm\_SyncChangeDir makes Commander change to the directory of the same name also in the other window  
\- [Find files](#bookmark=id.yr4hyk5v9h95): Start search inside an archive  
\- FTP: Option to [send keepalive messages](#bookmark=id.z1jkckxb8l8x) (e.g. NOOP) to the server in user-defined intervals (for max. 1 hour of inactivity)  
\- Support for packing of TAR/GZ/TGZ [archives](#bookmark=id.upoorj6vxv2x). Make sure to [choose the correct target OS](#bookmark=id.3k72qi5zcq4h) (Linux or SunOS).  
\- Direct packing of TAR.Plugin archives, requires re-download of the plugin (e.g. BZIP2)  
\- [Compare by contents](#bookmark=id.ds77z1uqv8jx): Search for text in both files simultaneously, found text will be underlined  
\- [Compare by contents](#bookmark=id.ds77z1uqv8jx): Button to show the two windows above each other, e.g. for wide texts  
\- Right click menu in [Lister](#bookmark=id.apj5cft08s6c): added "Copy all URLs" command in HTML-Viewer mode  
\- Pack: Option to [create a separate archive](#bookmark=id.6pn1v02nbu7) for each selected file/dir. If no target dir is given, the packed file will be placed in the same dir as the original file.  
\- "Branch view" now added to "commands" menu  
\- Create CRC-Checksum files in SFV format  
\- FTP+HTTP in background: Set speed limit for up- and downloads  
\- Pause button for background operations: FTP, HTTP, copy, pack, unpack  
\- FTP download from list: detect if list file was modified, and add new items to current download  
\- Download list can now also copy+move files.  
Syntax:   copy:sourcename \-\> targetname   or   move:sourcename \-\> targetname  
\- Background transfer manager can now also be started separately without a list file  
   
**New functions in Commander 4.54:**  
   
\- [Compare by content](#bookmark=id.q5tpjto68g9t): Switch between binary and text mode.  
\- Lister: Support word wrap in UTF-8 mode  
   
**New functions in Commander 4.53:**  
   
\- Display of UTF-8 (special 1-4 byte Unicode format) in [Lister](#bookmark=id.apj5cft08s6c)  
\- Support for ACE 2.0 [archives](#bookmark=id.upoorj6vxv2x)  
\- Support for files \> 2 GB in [Lister](#bookmark=id.apj5cft08s6c) and [split](#bookmark=id.5w5pgviztdzg)/[combine](#bookmark=id.jc8ggnqir4zt) functions  
\- Directory [print](#bookmark=id.lf85z2scy44t) with subdirs: Print only files of certain types, e.g. \*.txt \*.doc  
\- [Change date/time](#bookmark=id.26zryhc1nip5) of folders also on Windows NT/2000 (admins only due to restricted rights)  
\- [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7): Resume upload (binary files only). **WARNING:** With some versions of the server WarFTPd, the resume seems to work, but the uploaded file is unusable\!  
\- [Directory hotlist](#bookmark=id.56m1msgg5onh) can now contain up to 200 entries  
\- The location of [Wincmd.ini](#bookmark=id.183qx65tqgyw) and [Wcx\_ftp.ini](#bookmark=id.m2vgxhf7pr5h) can now be set in the registry (32-bit and 64-bit versions only):  
**\\SOFTWARE\\Ghisler\\Total Commander**, new text values IniFileName and FtpIniName.  
This key may be created under HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER or HKEY\_LOCAL\_MACHINE  
The [command line parameters](#bookmark=id.qvpuk8mmlsnj) /i= and /f= still take precedence over the registry values.  
\- Special larger block sizes when copying very large files can increase the copying speed of these large files quite a bit.  
This function is only meant for advanced users, and needs to be enabled through [wincmd.ini](#bookmark=id.183qx65tqgyw) (CopyBlockSize etc).  
\- Many small corrections and additions  
   
**New functions in Commander 4.52:**  
   
\- Display of Unicode and HTML (as plain text) in [Lister](#bookmark=id.apj5cft08s6c)  
\- Search for Unicode and Hex in the [search function](#bookmark=id.pr21tforgea1)  
\- [Print function](#bookmark=id.lf85z2scy44t) to print directory lists, trees and compare results in 'Synchronize dirs'.  
\- Display of all files in the current dir and all subdirs with **Ctrl+B**  
\- [File windows above each other](#bookmark=id.1gazo883hyjv) instead of side by side  
\- [Display of the file size](#bookmark=id.tkyukyx891k8) in kbytes or dynamic depending on the actual size  
\- [Multi-rename tool](#bookmark=id.glcyx4vx90yj): Enhanced counter settings using definition strings \[Cxxx\]  
\- Submenu 'New' in the right click context menu allows to create new (empty) files  
   
**Version 4.51 is a bugfix version of 4.50.**  
   
\- Bugfixes.  
   
**New functions in Commander 4.50:**  
   
\- [Multi-rename tool](#bookmark=id.glcyx4vx90yj): Allows to rename multiple files in one step (Hotkey: Ctrl+T)  
\- [Batch rename](#bookmark=id.ty2z2fwjlbfi) function with Shift+F6 to quickly rename multiple files one by one  
\- [Rename](#bookmark=id.ty2z2fwjlbfi) files and subdirs inside a ZIP archive (Shift+F6)  
\- [Parallel port transfer](#bookmark=id.9lna6uc3jvj8) function (direct cable connection), works between Win95/98/NT/2000/XP/Vista/7/3.1 and DOS\!  
\- FTP: Definition of [custom host types](#bookmark=id.r5cp5ajvcrzy), using a definition string  
\- [FTP: Retry to connect](#bookmark=id.wc2tebwbg2d9) multiple times also for non-anonymous connections  
\- FTP: Support for multiple proxies (separately for FTP and HTTP connections)  
\- FTP: Workaround to bug in some FTP servers: Upload of subdirs failed  
\- Resolve lnk files on the desktop or in the Network Neighborhood  
\- Unpack self-extracting files created by WinACE and WinRAR (open with Ctrl+PgDn)  
\- "Unpack all and execute" in packer properties allows to try out a program or run an installer from inside an archive  
\- [Define custom colors](#bookmark=id.kjcwrknoffrd) for different file types, e.g. all directories, all zip files etc.  
\- [Search for text](#bookmark=id.yr4hyk5v9h95) also inside CAB files  
\- [Copying](#bookmark=id.k5ygyj1h3gfr) to 'write only' directories (Windows NT, network)  
\- Uninstaller: Automatic removal of the program through the Control Panel  
Several new commands and parameters for [Button bar](#bookmark=id.let06d20891b) / [Start menu](#bookmark=id.hto08yjc25rh):  
\- cm\_List now allows to open a file. The file name must be given directly behind CM\_LIST, and not in the parameters field\!  
Example: cm\_list c:\\windows\\wincmd.ini always opens the file wincmd.ini in lister.  
\- cm\_ShowFileUser: Show which remote user has opened a local file (through a shared directory)  
\- cm\_EditPersmissionInfo: Show permissions dialog on Windows NT (NTFS file system)  
\- cm\_EditAuditInfo: Show file auditing dialog (NTFS)  
\- cm\_EditOwnerInfo: Show "Take ownership" dialog (NTFS)  
\- cm\_ShowOnlySelected: Hide all files/dirs which aren't selected when this function is used  
\- cm\_OpenRecycled: Open 'recycle bin'  
\- New parameters %L, %l, %F, %f, %D, %d create a list file in the TEMP directory with the names of the selected files and directories.  
   
Version 4.03 is a bugfix version of 4.02.  
   
**New functions in Commander 4.02:**  
   
\- Unzip, [delete](#bookmark=id.krhyvinhddnv) and HTTP downloads (Ctrl+N) in background.  
\- [Synchronize dirs](#bookmark=id.hc0qx9n0ylfr) now also supports directory from/to ftp synchronization\! Concerning the date/time synchronizing problems with ftp, please read the section ***important note*** on the page [Synchronize dirs](#bookmark=id.hc0qx9n0ylfr).  
\- Tray icon right click menu (context menu).  
\- Direct upload of files from inside an archive to an [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7) server.  
\- Better parsing of [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7) file lists downloaded via a HTTP proxy.  
\- [User-defined keyboard shortcuts](#bookmark=id.gfk42s7a5xco).  
\- Split "Equal/Unequal" button into two buttons in [synchronize](#bookmark=id.hc0qx9n0ylfr) function  
\- [Change date/time](#bookmark=id.d0g6wbu6rqt3) of directories  
\- [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7) server to server transfers (FXP): Always sends PORT command to left server, PASV to right server. This allows for file transfers between a public server and one in a private address room, or behind a firewall. The private server must be in the *left* window.  
\- [Find files:](#bookmark=id.pr21tforgea1) Only search in selected files and folders  
   
**Here is a list of the most important additions in Commander 4.0:**  
   
\- [Compare files by content](#bookmark=id.ds77z1uqv8jx)  
\- [Automatically adjust column width](#bookmark=id.tkyukyx891k8) of name column when resizing Commander  
\- Copy: rename file if target exists  
\- [Copy](#bookmark=id.k5ygyj1h3gfr) and [zip](#bookmark=id.9u33g0y0tace) in background (separate thread)  
\- [Synchronize](#bookmark=id.hc0qx9n0ylfr) directories with subdirs  
\- Bitmap viewer in [Lister](#bookmark=id.apj5cft08s6c), additional formats through Irfanview  
\- [Copy](#bookmark=id.k5ygyj1h3gfr) files directly from one archive to another  
\- [Restore selection](#bookmark=id.od2wg534aqtb) as it was before the last file operation (NUM /)  
\- [Extend right click menu](#bookmark=id.pucpl7ryocfu) (in association dialog)  
\- Add FTP files to list (through the [context menu](#bookmark=id.7hbnhy6khviy)), download later  
\- [Save configuration](#bookmark=id.p6z8h8111d35) through menu command  
\- Search for [duplicate files](#bookmark=id.lnoqmkwdjp2p)  
\- [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7): retry to connect if connection fails  
\- Skip files when copying and file doesn't fit on target disk  
\- Support WWW proxy for [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7)  
\- More detailed file display, e.g. only list/[select](#bookmark=id.od2wg534aqtb) files with certain dates and sizes  
\- [Select](#bookmark=id.od2wg534aqtb) files which do not match certain wildcards, e.g. all files except for programs  
\- More virtual folders, like the desktop, my computer etc. \- open through [button bar](#bookmark=id.let06d20891b)  
\- Wrap text at word boundaries in [lister](#bookmark=id.apj5cft08s6c)  
\- [Search](#bookmark=id.yr4hyk5v9h95) for files which do NOT contain a given text  
\- [Drive buttons](#bookmark=id.suaf8pw4apvp) separately per window  
\- Support for more FTP servers  
\- [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7): send specific commands directly after connecting  
\- [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7): Warn if binary file is transferred in text mode  
\- Icons for PIF files, virtual folders (directories having the system attribute set)  
\- [Search for hexadecimal](#bookmark=id.6eek5on62ik5) in lister  
\- [Quick search:](#bookmark=id.fhim3lcu0kjk) letters only but with quick search dialog  
\- Select [FTP](#bookmark=id.nqsl5o8cr6n7) transfer mode with keyboard (CTRL+SHIFT+M)  
\- Copy to NUL, PRN, LPTx, COMx  
\- CTRL+N or URL Button now allow to download files from WEB servers too  
\- Define your own hints for [drive names](#bookmark=id.it391ooe8i2p)  
\- Use an external icon library (ICL) to replace the default icons in the file lists. See [**www.ghisler.com**](http://www.ghisler.com/) for a sample ICL.  
\- Additional packers+unpackers can be added as extension DLLs (see [**www.ghisler.com**](http://www.ghisler.com/))  
\- Of course many small corrections and additions
